The Following are my observation about First Test, Day Two:   1) I thought India did well in the morning session. They hold the line; they neutralized England's attack and were about to take a strong position, but Rohit played that shot. Why Rohit Why?  2) Yes, I know this is his style, but he defies many test match logics. He played an aggressive shot right before lunch and played a shot in the air where the fielder was placed; I thought he played a Pakistani batsman shot.   3) Pujara & Rehane Looked Shell Shocked. They were behaving as it was their first test match. Pujara was leaving straight balls. However, I thought Pujara got too good of a ball. Usually, too good of a ball does not get a wicket, but Butler took a superb catch.  However, still, Pujara was looking walking wicket to me.   4) Having survived a close run out, what Rahane was thinking? He was taking a risky single in that kind of match situation. The ball was hit right in front of him. He could have also called no for it. Even if they run for that single, then Rahul was a goner.   5) Kohli got the straight-up good ball right in his weakness area. Kohli's batting form is a worrisome sign.   6) India got unlucky; they survive 46 overs, the ball was old, bowlers were tired a bit, they had a chance to score some easy runs, but rain ruins their day. Now on day three morning, Anderson will come fresh, hungry, full of confidence, and with his tail up.   7) Here are a few hunches of mine for discussion points of view.   -I felt Rahul looked satisfied with his runs. I think he will not make many runs on day 3. if he did, he would solidify his place in playing eleven.   -I will not trust Jadeja (I know he scored two fifties in the side match) or tailender for many runs.   -In my opinion, the game will revolve around Pant. The more he scores, the better position India will be in.   8) India has to get 275 to make England uncomfortable. I'm not expecting a big inning from England in the third innings, but chasing any score on the fourth inning on Trent Bridge stadium is not going to be easy. Even 150 could get tricky.
